2026-04-15 15:57:50.420 +03:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (1ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT o."Id", o."CreatedAt", o."Status", o."TotalPrice", u."Email", u."Id", s."ProductId", s."ProductName", s."Quantity", s."Price", s."Id", s."Id0"
FROM "Orders" AS o
INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON o."UserId" = u."Id"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT o0."ProductId", p."Name" AS "ProductName", o0."Quantity", o0."Price", o0."Id", p."Id" AS "Id0", o0."OrderId"
    FROM "OrderItems" AS o0
    INNER JOIN "Products" AS p ON o0."ProductId" = p."Id"
) AS s ON o."Id" = s."OrderId"
ORDER BY o."CreatedAt" DESC, o."Id", u."Id", s."Id"
